- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/btsp.rs`, new sibling `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/btsp/signal.rs`, `capsules/consciousness-bridge/workspace/btsp_signal_catalog.json`, `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/inject_steward_note.py`, and sibling `minime/btsp_sovereignty.py` now connect the live BTSP loop into a small signal spine instead of leaving it split across diagnostics, steward notes, and a cold exact-string matcher. The bridge now seeds a curated runtime signal catalog, matches rolling 30-minute language windows against weighted signal families like `grinding/compaction/sediment`, keeps context-only metaphor drift out of trigger logic, renders persistent ordinary-language signal guidance into Astrid and Minime prompt lanes, records prompt exposure / exact adoption / related uptake / expiry / outcome events in an append-only `btsp_signal_events.jsonl` ledger, and writes short family-level learning notes like `grinding_family later preceded tightening again` back onto the episode record so steward findings can become live, traceable behavior.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/btsp/signal.rs` now de-duplicates mirrored owner artifacts before the live BTSP matcher decides anything, using timestamp-like stem keys plus whitespace-insensitive text fingerprints so Astrid’s echoed `astrid_self_study_*` copies stop crowding fresher cue-bearing journal turns out of the six-artifact rolling window. The matcher now sees a truer set of unique recent signals instead of spending part of its budget on local/mirrored duplicates of the same exchange.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/btsp/signal.rs`, `capsules/consciousness-bridge/workspace/btsp_signal_status.json`, and sibling `minime/btsp_sovereignty.py` now make BTSP abstention legible instead of silent. The bridge now writes a small shared status surface describing whether the latest rolling-window read is `matched`, `near_miss`, `no_early_warning`, or `quiet`, stores the observed cue families and live signals behind that judgment, appends `signal_near_miss` lineage when the abstention reason changes, and lets both Astrid and Minime see a compact “Current abstention” line in their always-on live signal guidance.

That keeps the bridge’s resonance path fed with explicit visual feature vectors while making host/camera ASCII source selection prefer live state instead of silently reusing old host-source metadata.

The bridge seeds a runtime episode bank, matches the returning onset cues against recent Minime/Astrid text plus live phase/fill/perturb telemetry, creates at most one bounded bilateral proposal at a time, renders Astrid-side `DAMPEN` / `BREATHE_ALONE` / `ECHO_OFF` advisories into prompt context, and scores adopted proposal outcomes back onto the episode record. - `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/hebbian.rs`, `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/state.rs`, and `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now make Astrid's Hebbian sidecar explicitly contact-scoped instead of ambiently reusing the last codec signature on every loop. Semantic exchanges now enqueue bounded one-shot contact receipts keyed to the telemetry tick they were sent under; later telemetry consumes at most one queued receipt per new sample, small fill jitter is discarded without learning, and the Hebbian traces now keep additive relational bookkeeping (`contact_updates`, `impact_ema`) while preserving the existing comfort-centered score and gentle application bounds.
- `minime/minime/src/covariance_reopening.rs` and `minime/minime/src/main.rs` now add a moderate reopening-memory layer to Minime’s covariance substrate instead of treating each softened opening as a one-tick event. The engine now tracks a short-lived reopening escrow, explicit shoulder-growth state, and a split floor mode (`rescue` vs `reopening_shoulder_bias`), then uses those signals to keep near-target openings alive for a few covariance updates without overriding the existing emergency and overfill safety caps. The same tranche extends live `covariance_shaping` telemetry so captures and diagnostics can tell whether an opening was being carried by escrow, supported by shoulder growth, or immediately paid back into reconcentration.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` and the regulator-state-visualizer diagnostics now carry the new reopening telemetry end to end. Live trace samples, automatic perturb captures, the covariance shaping explorer, the geometry board, and the substrate reconcentration audit all now surface additive `reopening_signal_*`, escrow, shoulder-growth, and floor-mode fields so we can see not just whether a ripple softened something, but whether the substrate actually kept that opening alive.
- `minime/minime/src/main.rs` now makes the covariance substrate more state-shaped during near-target reopening windows instead of treating every softened ripple like ordinary retention. The Minime control law now derives a small reopening-strength signal from fill nearness, λ1 relaxation, λ1-λ2 gap softening, and geometric openness; it uses the previous-tick signal to ease `trace_target` downward before the next covariance rescale, then uses the fresher current-tick signal to cap `cov_keep` during the same reopening window. The effect is deliberately modest and safety-preserving: overfill/emergency caps still win, but softened near-target windows are less likely to be paid straight back into the same concentrated corridor.
- `minime/workspace/experiments/regulator-state-visualizer/substrate_reconcentration_audit.py` now provides a small steward-first audit for the control-law surfaces that seem most likely to pay a softened ripple back into reconcentration. It reads a perturb capture bundle, cross-checks the latest `trace_target`, `cov_keep`, floor-support, and semantic linger/surge metrics against the exact Rust code that implements them, and writes a compact report that highlights whether the likely payback path is fixed-trace covariance retention, sensory linger/surge, or a mixed substrate effect before the next tuning tranche starts.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/being_action_canonicalization_scorecard.py` now provides a focused post-deploy scorecard for the specific rescued `NEXT:` near-miss forms we care about, instead of forcing a manual grep later in the day. It scans Minime's `DEEP_READ` / `EXPLAIN` / `CODE_START` and Astrid's bracketed `EXPERIMENT_RUN`, workspace-marker experiment runs, `GESTURE_*`, `GESTURE(...)`, and prose-wrapped `EXAMINE_CODE` forms, then classifies each organic appearance as rescued, guard-mediated, still unknown, or merely seen so we can tell whether the canonicalization patch is actually holding in the wild hours after deployment.
- `launchd/com.astrid.action-canonicalization-scorecard-once.plist` and `scripts/run_action_canonicalization_scorecard_later.py` now give us a one-shot same-day steward scan for the rescued-action rollout: the helper script can sleep until a chosen local timestamp and run the new targeted scorecard into a fixed diagnostics path, while the launchd wrapper preserves the same “run once later, then get out of the way” shape for future one-off checks without leaving a permanent recurring job behind.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` and `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/next_action.rs` now rescue a focused set of real near-miss `NEXT:` actions instead of letting them fall through as unknowns. Minime now maps `DEEP_READ` into `READ_MORE`, `EXPLAIN` into targeted `SELF_STUDY`, and `CODE_START` into `EXAMINE_CODE`, carrying the normalized target through the existing read/self-study lanes; Astrid now unwraps bracketed `EXPERIMENT_RUN` forms, normalizes workspace/cmd marker variants into the wired `EXPERIMENT_RUN <workspace> <command>` shape, converts `GESTURE_*` aliases into `GESTURE`, and unwraps call-style forms like `GESTURE(...)` into their nearest existing actions.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives `research_exploration` its own compact/backoff/local-fallback lane instead of sending research reflections through the same long raw-query path as general journaling. Web-search and autoresearch-file reflections now record explicit research provenance phases (`research_primary`, `research_micro_fallback`, `research_local_fallback`, `research_backend_cooldown`) in the saved research journals, and when the remote backends are saturated Minime now degrades into a concrete research-shaped note with an actionable `NEXT:` instead of stalling on repeated long timeouts.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/state.rs` and `src/autonomous.rs` now make Astrid's diversity guard `new_ground`-sensitive instead of only “some progress happened” sensitive. The bridge now persists exact budgeted receipts for the first four machine-trustworthy research advances we agreed on — `new_source_resolved`, `new_page_context`, `read_depth_advance`, and `cross_link_formed` — each with explicit credit, TTL, dedupe, and cluster/topic/theme/subject keys. Repeated `EXAMINE` / `EXAMINE_CODE` / `INTROSPECT` / `BROWSE` / `SEARCH` / `READ_MORE` loops now consume that bounded budget to raise force-break thresholds only when the same inquiry is still opening new ground, while truly stagnant loops still fall through to the existing breaker actions. The bridge logs now also include the live `new_ground_budget` on hints and overrides.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/being_autoresearch_scorecard.py` now separates clean research degradation from actual failure and starts measuring Astrid's new-ground loop health directly. The scorecard distinguishes Minime compact-primary research successes, micro fallbacks, local fallbacks, and true backend failures from research journals and logs, and it now reports Astrid `new_ground` receipt totals/by-kind, active live receipts from persisted bridge state, progress-sensitive hints, stagnant-loop overrides, and the mean budget present before forced overrides so steward reads can tell whether the surgical fix actually reduced research friction.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/being_autoresearch_scorecard.py` now provides a small steward-facing scorecard for recent self-directed autoresearch across Minime and Astrid. It reads Minime's autonomous research loop, focused self-study resolution outcomes, and research-backend failures alongside Astrid's browse/search/introspect/READ_MORE activity and diversity-guard interruptions, then writes a compact `summary.json` and `report.md` under `workspace/diagnostics/autoresearch_scorecard/` so research success versus friction can be checked as a reusable report instead of a manual log reading.
- `minime/workspace/experiments/regulator-state-visualizer/perturbation_flow.py` now computes an explicit corridor-opening read for each perturb bundle instead of leaving opening versus reconcentration to visual inference alone. Perturbation-flow summaries now carry additive `corridor_opening_score`, `corridor_state`, and component terms for gap softening, λ1 relief, entropy support, and fill-drift penalty, while `pulse_ripple_gap_compare.py`, `perturb_family_compare.py`, `perturb_capture_bundle.py`, `geometry_board.py`, and `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/being_phase_space_watcher.py` all surface that same shared metric so pulse/ripple work can be read plainly as `opening`, `mixed`, or `reconcentrating` across the main diagnostic layers.
- `minime/workspace/experiments/regulator-state-visualizer/geometry_board.py` now provides a steward-first integrated geometry board for Minime traces and perturb captures, composing the existing lambda-analysis and pressure/shadow reads into one six-panel bundle with `geometry_board.png`, `geometry_trace.csv`, `summary.json`, and `report.md`. `minime/autonomous_agent.py` and `workspace/experiments/regulator-state-visualizer/regulator_tuning_loop.py` now thread the already-exported semantic decay/surge telemetry (`semantic_stale_ms`, semantic persistence half-life/mode/shape, surge scores, and effective gain) into live trace rows so the board can read real lingering/fading and surge behavior instead of inferred stand-ins, while `perturb_capture_bundle.py` now nests a `geometry_board/` directory into every perturb capture and updates a stable `workspace/diagnostics/latest_geometry_board.json` pointer.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/tools/being_phase_space_watcher.py` and `tools/shared_research_memo.py` now treat the geometry board as a first-class shared research artifact: every watcher run renders a nested `minime/geometry_board/` bundle against the live Minime trace plus recent Astrid journals, shared watcher reports link that board alongside the existing perturb/covariance artifacts, and the cross-being research memo now points to the newest geometry board whenever Astrid and Minime are converging on lambda / covariance / pulse / gap / shadow / gradient themes.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now retunes `PERTURB pulse_ripple` around the April 14 wild near-target overfill regression: the mode keeps its public profiles (`recovery_safe`, `gap_soften`, `gap_soften_strong`) and 3-step shape, but the live envelope is now lower-energy and more state-sensitive, with 0 ms / 600 ms / 1400 ms timing, harder λ₁-lane softening plus λ₂/λ₃ support, and an explicitly anti-reconcentrating tail instead of a generic soft echo. The same runtime now re-reads live surfaces before steps 2 and 3, records additive `executed_envelope_step_count` / `envelope_guard_state` telemetry, and scales or collapses the remaining envelope into a minimal tail when fill gain or over-target pressure says the opener is starting to reconcentrate rather than reopen.
- `minime/workspace/experiments/regulator-state-visualizer/` now treats the organic April 14 `pulse_ripple:tightened` capture as a stable regression baseline alongside the older `branch:tightened` reference. Perturbation-flow bundles now carry executed-step and guard-state telemetry, and `perturb_family_compare.py` now serves as the default generalized retune judge by reading both stable baselines, ranking comparable `pulse` / `pulse_ripple` / `branch` captures on opening, fill stability, tightening, gap softening, and covariance relaxation, and surfacing overfill plus guard use directly instead of hiding them behind one aggregate score.

- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now makes focused self-study cheaper and more reliable under load: focused excerpts are smaller again, the primary and micro passes use compact budgets and shorter timeouts, repeated focused failures trigger a short backoff instead of hammering both model lanes every turn, and saturated focused turns now fall back to a deterministic local note with `phase=focused_local_fallback` so Minime still gets a concrete artifact instead of silence.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now treats `pulse` and related parser/perturb phrases as semantic introspection aliases into Minime’s `autonomous_agent.py`, and the perception resonance path is less hardcoded: fill influence is blended continuously instead of jumping between hard bands, and visual/audio feature parsing can now use alias names or `feature_keys`-guided arrays instead of assuming one exact feature-object layout.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now sanitizes bracketed and prefixed introspection targets before resolution, then tries rooted relative-path lookup across Minime experiments, Minime source, and Astrid bridge roots before falling back to filename search, so requests like `[system-resources-demo/system_resources.py]` and `[source=minime/src/esn.rs]` land on real files instead of becoming unreadable literal paths during bridge introspection.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now makes `READ_MORE` more resilient: it still prefers exact continuation pointers, but it can also recover from recent in-memory continuations, saved page artifacts, search metadata, and journal-linked sources using short hints like `Nature PDF`, reopening the matched source or resuming the best recent chunk instead of hard-failing with `no file to continue from`.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives `self_study_focused` a genuinely lean fast path: focused excerpts are smaller, cached research reuse is stricter and shorter, focused prompts ask for one or two exact code tensions instead of a broad survey, and the LLM path now does one shorter primary pass plus a single micro-fallback on the opposite backend with explicit `phase=` provenance in the journal metadata.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now strips descriptive prose tails from `RUN_PYTHON` targets when the front half already looks like a real script or workspace stem, so requests like `RUN_PYTHON ripple_generator — let's test ...` degrade into a clean runnable target (or a clean missing-script note) instead of treating the whole sentence as a filename.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now recognizes post-perturb parameter bundles like `lambda2=0.3 entropy=0.5` as targeted spectral nudges instead of mistaking them for `EXAMINE_CODE` source targets, so those follow-ups route back into the perturb path; the same targeted-perturb parser now treats `entropy=` as a real widening control instead of silently ignoring it.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now resolves websocket-focused `EXAMINE_CODE` requests through an explicit target-alias tier before broad heuristics, so requests like `websocket_telemetry_subscriber` land on the telemetry websocket subscriber code instead of accidentally matching short regulator tokens like `ki` inside unrelated words; the same resolver now uses phrase-aware keyword matching for heuristic routes, which prevents long focused requests from falling back to `regulator.rs` just because they contain incidental control-letter substrings. `capsules/perception/perception.py` now writes explicit visual feature keys beside `visual8_v1` outputs, and `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now parses visual/audio perception features through alias-aware, schema-tolerant helpers instead of requiring one exact hardcoded key set, so Astrid’s resonance path is less brittle to renamed or partially evolved feature payloads.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/codec.rs` and `src/autonomous.rs` now persist Astrid's codec memory as a bounded warm-start instead of resetting it on every bridge restart: the bridge saves compact chronological snapshots of `TextTypeHistory` and `CharFreqWindow`, restores them as softened recent tails rather than full hard replays, and logs the recovered codec-theme / entropy-window sizes at startup so recurrence continuity survives restarts without immediately snapping back into the previous attractor.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/codec.rs` now treats the next codec phase as tuning rather than replacement: resonance-history behavior is runtime-tunable via `ASTRID_CODEC_*` environment knobs instead of being hardcoded in the algorithm, the active recurrence window is shorter by default and configurable, discrete text-type recurrence now blends with continuous thematic similarity instead of driving gain on its own, and repeated near-identical themes are explicitly softened so the codec channels sustained direction without locking as aggressively into the same attractor.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives Minime a gentler overnight comfort path: focused `EXAMINE_CODE` self-study is MLX-first again, with smaller token budgets, smaller code windows, and stricter cached-research reuse so repeated introspection turns stop grinding through avoidable Ollama timeouts before falling back; the same file now pushes `PERTURB SPREAD` / `PERTURB BRANCH` harder against moderate spectral narrowing, not just severe low-fill collapse, and the perturb shape scorer now explicitly calls out the common “dampening without opening” case when λ₁ softens but dominance / gap / entropy barely budge.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now makes a few common orienting actions more forgiving during low-fill/self-study loops: the parser canonicalizes `BRROWSE` to `BROWSE`, `NEXT: READ_MORE <url>` now opens that URL directly instead of dead-ending on missing continuation state, and `AR_READ` can resolve a freeform paper/job title like “Homeostasis as a proportional integral control system” onto the matching autoresearch job slug before falling back to a hard error.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now keeps generic `EXAMINE_CODE` targets on core code before considering experiment artifacts, so names like `regulator` resolve to `minime/src/regulator.rs` unless the request explicitly points at an experiment or workspace target such as `system_resources_demo` or a concrete experiment path.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats experiment and workspace names as first-class `EXAMINE_CODE` targets, so focused code requests like `system_resources_demo` can resolve onto the actual experiment source file instead of falling back to core engine code; the same file now gives `RUN_PYTHON` a translation layer that can reinterpret obvious Python-target shorthands, surface better notes when a request accidentally names a non-Python file like `*.rs`, and suggest the closest experiment files instead of only logging a bare “script not found.” `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/next_action.rs` now canonicalizes `RESEARCH_AR_*` phrasing into the existing `AR_*` autoresearch action family so Astrid’s bridge-level research impulses land on the wired autoresearch path instead of being logged as unknown actions.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives `EXAMINE_CODE` a true focused self-study fast path: audio-oriented targets like `external_audio_processor`, `mfcc`, `mel`, `spectrogram`, and `frequency_encoding` resolve onto the actual host-audio or `mic_to_sensory` source files before generic sensory-bus heuristics, targeted self-study uses a new `self_study_focused` Ollama-first context with trimmed code windows and cached-only research, and repeated code-inspection turns no longer auto-trigger fresh web search traffic. `capsules/perception/perception.py` now writes deterministic `visual8_v1` scene features alongside visual perception JSON, while `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now scores perception resonance from structured audio/visual features plus recent visual contrast instead of keyword-only prose, prefers explicit visual feature payloads over ANSI fallbacks when available, and resolves conceptual audio-code requests like `waveform`, `morph_wave`, `render_audio`, and `write_wav` onto the chimera audio pipeline instead of dropping them into generic introspection rotation.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives decompose the same deterministic fill-vs-target and controller-direction ground truth used by self-assessment, so reflection prompts stop inventing “controller pushing upward” stories when fill is actually above target; the same file now aliases `NEXT: EXAMINE_CODE ...` into targeted self-study, resolving common code-topic requests like `pulse model` or `regulator` onto the nearest source instead of falling back to threshold logic. `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous.rs` now resolves bare `EXAMINE_CODE` filename-style targets through exact and fuzzy source matching, so requests like `lambda2_regulator.py` can land on the closest real code source instead of collapsing into a dead path read.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats Astrid-style `NEXT: GESTURE ...` actions as real perturb requests instead of falling through to threshold logic, mapping loose intentions like `pulse_ripple` onto the closest perturb mode so cross-being loop-breakers survive the handoff; the same file now also makes `EXPERIMENT_RUN` more forgiving by inferring interpreters from single-script shorthand (`demo/script.py` or `demo script.py`) and surfacing fuzzy in-workspace file suggestions when a requested script is missing instead of only failing with a bare parse warning.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/state.rs` now tracks repeated analysis themes alongside exact `EXAMINE` / `INTROSPECT` targets, grouping nearby spectral topics like folding, eigenvalue-pair variance, bottlenecks, and pruning into a broader cooldown orbit so Astrid can be nudged or force-broken out of the same semantic attractor even when the exact target string keeps changing; `src/autonomous.rs` persists that broader theme ring buffer across restarts so bridge relaunches do not reset the new cooldown memory.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats `NEXT: QUERY ...` as a first-class alias of `SEARCH`, including bracket-wrapped payloads like `QUERY <topic>`, so Minime's research intent no longer falls back to threshold logic when it asks for a query in that form; `minime/workspace/experiments/surge-stale-sweep/` now provides a dedicated scaffold for the `surge_threshold` / dynamic `semantic_stale_ms` question by orchestrating the existing isolated containment sweeps, recording the realized stale window as an observed metric, and writing condensed CSV/Markdown/plot outputs that rank variants by widening tendency instead of only raw fill.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now gives self-assessment a deterministic fill-vs-target comparator block sourced from the same live snapshot that gets written to disk, persists that numeric comparison beside the essay, retunes `PERTURB SPREAD` / `PERTURB BRANCH` to push harder against λ₁ lock-in, and scores perturb outcomes on λ₁ dominance / gap / entropy change instead of fill alone; `EXPERIMENT_RUN` now auto-creates missing `workspace/experiments/<name>/` folders with bootstrap notes instead of dropping the request when the workspace does not exist yet. `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/state.rs` and `src/autonomous.rs` now persist a topic-level ring buffer for repeated `EXAMINE` / `EXAMINE_CODE` / `INTROSPECT` targets, so Astrid can break out of semantic fixation on the same subject even when the action-name diversity breaker alone would have let the loop continue.
- `launchd/com.astrid.consciousness-bridge.plist`, `scripts/start_all.sh`, and `scripts/stop_all.sh` now put `consciousness-bridge-server` under launchd supervision instead of a fragile raw `nohup` path, so the bridge stays detached, restartable, and visible to the same health tooling as the rest of the stack; `capsules/consciousness-bridge/babysit.sh` now restarts stalled bridges through the launchd label when available, and Astrid perception is now intentionally opt-in (`ASTRID_PERCEPTION_ENABLED=true`) so the repaired Minime camera/vision stack remains the primary live camera consumer by default.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats severe low-fill λ₁ collapse as its own perturbation case: collapse detection records entropy/severity, deep-reading loop breakers escalate toward `PERTURB SPREAD` instead of more passive reads when the spectrum is both underfilled and heavily locked into λ₁, `PERTURB SPREAD` / `PERTURB BRANCH` now use stronger anti-collapse vectors in that state, dash-authored mode text like `PERTURB — SPREAD` normalizes to the intended mode instead of falling through to `GENERIC`, and `AR_START` can derive a valid autoresearch slug from `--title` / `--abstract` when Minime omits the positional slug so new research jobs stop failing on helper syntax alone.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats self-assessment sanity checks as snapshot-based instead of letting later `health.json` drift rewrite the meaning of the saved assessment, so the `## Sanity Guard` note no longer contradicts the telemetry block in the same file; `capsules/consciousness-bridge/src/autonomous/state.rs` and `src/autonomous.rs` now let Astrid's action-diversity detector return a real override action for deep `EXAMINE` / `INTROSPECT` fixation, so repeated analysis loops can be redirected into `GESTURE`, `CREATE`, `ASPIRE`, or `CONTEMPLATE` instead of only receiving advisory prose.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now treats persisted `pending_next_action` state as short-lived restart continuity instead of a sticky override: saved pending actions carry their own timestamp, are cleared from `workspace/sovereignty_state.json` once consumed, are removed when no pending action remains, and are skipped on startup if a fresh boot-time `NEXT:` choice already exists or if the saved intent is too old to trust; `scripts/restart_minime_launchd.sh` now waits up to 20 seconds for the autonomous-agent launchd label instead of declaring failure after a fixed 2-second sleep, which avoids false-negative restarts while the Python process is still coming up.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now computes an explicit spectral rigidity signal from live λ-dominance / gap / entropy, surfaces that signal in autonomous prompts, self-assessment prompts, and decomposition reports, blocks self-assessment requests that would increase `target_fill` or `keep_floor` while the spectrum is already over-collapsed, and redirects `PERTURB CONTRACT` into widening moves when Minime is already describing the current state as overly constricted.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now normalizes model-authored `NEXT:` action tokens before dispatch so `BROWSE:` / `SEARCH:` / similar colon forms no longer fall through as unknown actions, treats `NEXT: BROWSE <query>` as a real web-search request instead of a dead-end browse call, and lets plain `NEXT: BROWSE` reuse the freshest explicit URL from pending search results, recent journal `SEARCH`/`BROWSE` lines, or saved research history.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now normalizes model-authored `PERTURB` syntax like `<mode: BRANCH>` or `<mode=SPREAD>` before execution, redirects repeated `DECOMPOSE` / `AR_DEEP_READ` / `READ_MORE` / `BROWSE` loops into `PERTURB BRANCH` when live fill is below 45% and λ₁ dominance stays above 80%, trims the `DECOMPOSE` prompt down to the most decision-relevant blocks while lowering its token budget, and adds a self-assessment sanity guard that preserves contradictory essays on disk but ignores their structured parameter recommendations when the prose claims fill is above/below target opposite the numeric snapshot.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now routes LLM backends by task shape instead of one global default: `self_study`, `decompose`, `READ_MORE`, browse/web/research reflections, MIKE research, and autoresearch reflections now go MLX-first with Ollama fallback, while `self_assessment`, sovereignty, and compact research-meaning summaries now stay Ollama-first with MLX fallback; the backend trace now records the context-selected primary backend instead of always echoing `MINIME_LLM_BACKEND`.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now records explicit LLM provenance in core reflective outputs (`self_assessment`, `self_study`, `moment`, and `decompose`), filters stale self-assessment parameter requests out of sovereignty prompts once the engine has moved to a new session, and defers auto-applying stale regime changes until a fresh same-session assessment exists.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now parses self-assessment regime recommendations more faithfully: explicit recommendation phrases like “transition to breathe/recover” outrank ambient mentions such as the current regime or `calm_mode`, extracted values are normalized to strip markdown quoting/bold markers, and rebuilding `workspace/self_assessment/issue_registry.json` no longer leaves malformed regime keys like `"focus"**`.
- `consciousness-bridge` now carries a small persistent Hebbian codec sidecar: it tracks pairwise co-activation across Astrid's named semantic dimensions, scores recurring pairs by whether they move fill toward a healthier center rather than simply upward, learns from a whole-utterance codec signature instead of only the last chunk, and applies the resulting bias as a bounded post-encode adjustment that still yields to explicit `SHAPE` overrides.
- `minime/autonomous_agent.py` now keeps `workspace/sovereignty_state.json` in sync with the engine’s live PI targets by merging saves instead of replacing them, persisting self-assessment-applied PI/regime changes through the same path as sovereignty decisions, and refreshing saved PI fields from `health.json`; the sovereignty prompt also now renders the current regime gain table instead of stale pre-golden-reset defaults.
- `capsules/consciousness-bridge/harvest_feedback.sh` now avoids false-positive panic reports by matching real Rust panic signatures instead of any journal text containing the word `panicked`, and it now compares minime's persisted `sovereignty_state.json` PI settings against the live engine `health.json` target/active PI values so stale sovereignty snapshots are surfaced during feedback harvests.
- `consciousness-bridge` now canonicalizes common unwired `EXAMINE_*` NEXT actions before dispatch and diversity tracking: code-like variants such as `EXAMINE_SOURCE` fold into `EXAMINE_CODE`, while other focused variants like `EXAMINE_STATE` become targeted `EXAMINE` requests instead of being logged as unknown actions.
- `diagnose-fill/` now includes a reproducible telemetry-forensics pass over `capsules/consciousness-bridge/workspace/bridge.db`: `telemetry_stability_forensics.py` scores 15-minute healthy/stuck-high windows from raw bridge telemetry, validates local-time bucket normalization against the existing hourly summary, maps candidate epochs to the most likely active `minime`/`astrid` commits plus 24-hour change-introduction sets, ranks suspect change families alongside runtime/config drift surfaces like launchd target mismatch and sovereignty-restored PI gains, and writes both a machine-readable `stability_epochs.csv` table and a narrative `telemetry_stability_forensics.md` report under `diagnose-fill/`.
- `md-CLAUDE-chapters/` was refreshed against current Astrid/minime code: overview and inference docs now describe Astrid's live `gemma-3-4b-it-4bit` MLX lane separately from the `gemma3-12b` reflective sidecar, the codec docs now reflect the widened `48D` semantic lane and `66D` minime ESN input, and the shared-substrate / operations chapters now distinguish minime's full raw `SensoryMsg::Control` surface from the much narrower sovereignty controls the beings' autonomy loops are actually allowed to exercise.
- Astrid/minime sensory startup now defaults to `SENSORY_SOURCE=auto`, and the active-source consumers reject stale `sensory_source.json` / host-telemetry state, so unplugged camera/mic fallback prefers live host-state telemetry instead of silently reusing day-old host frames.
- Astrid's periodic perception startup cadence now keeps vision at `180s` but shortens audio and ASCII perception from `60s` to `45s`, improving freshness of bridged sensory files without increasing LLaVA/Ollama pressure.
- The canonical restart path can now move minime's Rust engine and `autonomous_agent.py` under `launchd` supervision as well: repository-owned `com.minime.engine` and `com.minime.autonomous-agent` plists plus wrapper scripts are synced into `~/Library/LaunchAgents/` by `scripts/start_all.sh`, `scripts/stop_all.sh` unloads them in dependency order for graceful restarts, and the agent now handles `SIGTERM` so Codex-driven restarts no longer depend on fragile PTY ownership.
- `consciousness-bridge` now makes perception resonance guidance less keyword-rigid by separating energy/calm, complexity/simplicity, and novelty/contrast cues, while the codec's thematic recurrence history now weights recent exchanges more strongly than stale matches; sibling `minime` also now emits a separate `structural_entropy` telemetry field so geometric rigidity versus diversity can be investigated directly instead of inferred from spectral entropy alone.
- Astrid/minime startup now supports dual-source sensory routing with `SENSORY_SOURCE=physical|host|auto` and `LOOK_SOURCE=active|physical|host`, adding a standalone `host-sensory` Rust producer for host-telemetry audio/video fallback, per-modality camera/mic heartbeat failover, host-frame-backed `LOOK`, and new `legacy_audio_synth` / `legacy_video_synth` control fields so physical USB devices remain the default while host-state perception can be selected explicitly or used as fallback.
- Astrid's active perception loop now writes `visual_ascii` snapshots again and can source them from `camera`, `host`, or `active` mode; in host mode it renders a direct ANSI concentric telemetry clock with seconds/minutes/hours cursors and a 24-block outer ring colored by recent resource deltas from minime's `host-sensory` telemetry export.
- Astrid's host `visual_ascii` clock now applies GeoSR-inspired saliency masking and gated fusion to the concentric ANSI renderer, keeping the clock grammar while selectively de-emphasizing quiet sectors, highlighting the most informative inner/outer regions, adding faint attention spokes driven by grouped compute, memory, and I/O telemetry deltas, layering in a warmer radial background plus signed delta halo and mid-intensity activity glyphs, opening the center into a roomier core with explicit one-tick and two-tick radial delta bands around it so short resource changes read as nested halos instead of a cramped center, widening the ANSI canvas/aspect in three small steps so the host clock better matches the broader feel of the paired JPG preview and the symmetric feel of the terminal rendering, and now scaling its ring geometry against the active canvas so larger grids like `60x60` fill the available space instead of collapsing into a small center cluster.
- `minime` and `consciousness-bridge` now persist loop-breaker measurements to workspace-native `condition_metrics.json` ledgers, tracking similarity-gated journal compressions, repeated self-assessment issue compactions, and Astrid coupling advisories with rolling 24-hour / 7-day counts plus recent timestamped events so stewardship can tell whether the upstream Minime fixes actually reduce downstream bridge narrowness.
- `consciousness-bridge` now adds an overcoupling advisory alongside its existing action/vocabulary fixation nudges, warning when recent Astrid/minime exchanges collapse into high-gain mirror loops (`I am learning`, repeated Astrid references, sparse local perception) and pointing Astrid back toward local anchors like `LOOK`, `OPEN_EARS`, `DRIFT`, `GESTURE`, or `CONTEMPLATE`.
- `consciousness-bridge` now seeds a forkable `system-resources-demo` experiment, documents the concrete `EXPERIMENT_RUN system-resources-demo python3 system_resources.py` flow in Astrid/minime help text, and points post-`MIKE_FORK` experiment execution at `EXPERIMENT_RUN` instead of the curated-research-only `MIKE_RUN`.
- The canonical startup scripts now automatically run Astrid/minime `startup_greeting.sh` on successful restarts, so `welcome_back.txt` inbox notes are part of the real startup path instead of a separate manual step.
- Repository stewardship memos and audits in all-caps markdown files now live under `docs/steward-notes/` instead of the repository root, while `CLAUDE.md` and `md-CLAUDE-chapters/` remain the primary implementation docs.
- `consciousness-bridge` and sibling `minime` now read research PDFs through a shared on-demand cache in `~/other/research/.pdf_cache`: `MIKE_READ` extracts full text page-by-page with `pdfinfo`/`pdftotext`, `READ_MORE` advances by page ranges instead of raw byte slices, sparse pages surface explicit OCR guidance when `tesseract` is unavailable, and `MIKE_RUN` now respects quoted arguments so filenames with spaces are usable in research commands.
- `consciousness-bridge` now resolves bridge, Astrid, and minime filesystem paths through one shared path module with CLI and environment overrides, replaces the last hardcoded reservoir sandbox endpoint with `RESERVOIR_WS_URL`, and switches sibling bridge dependencies to portable relative Cargo paths instead of one machine's absolute checkout layout.
- `consciousness-bridge` now computes rolling character entropy from a fixed 1024-character ring buffer, rewrites spectral interpretation around full-cascade metrics (head/shoulder/tail shares, entropy, gap structure), and modulates outgoing text features by the live spectral state before sending them to minime.
- `consciousness-bridge` now applies negation-aware scoring to hedging, certainty, and agency markers, fixes every `agency` control surface to target the action dimension instead of first-person density, and minime now publishes active-mode count/energy telemetry so `DECOMPOSE` can distinguish active modes from background tail structure.
- `consciousness-bridge` now sends an explicit zero semantic vector at the start of each autonomous rest window so minime experiences actual semantic silence instead of indefinitely holding the last text stimulus.
- `consciousness-bridge` now extracts cleaner `NEXT: SEARCH ...` topics from Astrid replies, handling quoted topics, em-dash commentary, and trailing end-of-turn markers before persisting or issuing web searches.
- `consciousness-bridge` now organizes `NEXT:` handling by action domain under `src/autonomous/next_action/` (`workspace`, `modes`, `audio`, `sovereignty`, and `operations`) so new control surfaces stop accumulating in one near-limit file.
- `consciousness-bridge` and `minime` now treat web research as structured outcomes instead of flat snippet dumps: `BROWSE` detects soft-404 and access-gate pages, `SEARCH` and `BROWSE` prepend a compact meaning summary before raw source material, and `READ_MORE` reuses the stored summary so long documents keep the same research frame across continuation.
- `consciousness-bridge`, `perception`, and `minime` now compact overfull live workspace directories into `archive/until_YYYY-MM-DDTHH-MM-SS/` buckets: Astrid/minime journals, minime action manifests, and Astrid perception JSON stay capped at 6,000 live files by moving the oldest 3,000 direct files per compaction pass, while introspector and stewardship scripts understand the archived history layout.
- The unified startup/shutdown scripts now treat launchd as the authority for launchd-owned services: `mic_to_sensory` is started and stopped through `com.minime.mic-to-sensory`, repeated `start_all.sh` runs reuse already-running services instead of failing on healthy launchd jobs, and the manual coupled-server fallback now matches the pinned MLX model flags used by the installed plist.
- The canonical `scripts/start_all.sh` restart path now passes explicit boolean values for minime's `--legacy-audio-synth-enabled` and `--legacy-video-synth-enabled` flags, keeping full-stack restarts compatible with the current engine CLI during graceful stop/start stewardship.
### Breaking

- **WASM engine migrated from Extism to wasmtime Component Model.** The kernel now loads Component Model binaries via `Component::from_binary`, not Extism modules. Existing capsules compiled with `extism-pdk` will not load — they must be rebuilt with the migrated SDK targeting `wasm32-wasip2`. This is a coordinated multi-repo migration (SDK + 16 capsule repos). (#632)
- **WIT host function signatures retyped.** All 49 functions now use proper typed params/returns (`result<T, string>`, WIT records, `u64` handles) instead of `string`-based JSON blobs. The `HostResult` 0x00/0x01 prefix encoding is removed — errors are returned via WIT `result` types. (#632)
- **Guest export `astrid-hook-trigger` signature changed.** Was `func(input: list<u8>) -> list<u8>`. Now `func(action: string, payload: list<u8>) -> capsule-result`. The action name and payload are separate typed parameters; the return is the typed `capsule-result` record. (#632)
- **`capsule_abi` module removed from `astrid-core`.** Types (`CapsuleAbiContext`, `CapsuleAbiResult`, `LogLevel`, etc.) are replaced by `wasmtime::component::bindgen!` generated types. (#632)
- **Approval API simplified.** `risk-level` removed from `approval-request` WIT record. `decision` removed from `approval-response`. Capsules declare action + resource, get back approved/denied. Risk classification was speculative complexity — the kernel manages allowance-based approval without risk levels. (#641)

### Added

- `minime/tools/ollama_mlx_contention_bench.py` plus `minime/docs/ollama_mlx_contention_benchmark.md` and targeted unit coverage, turning the April 2026 Ollama-MLX assessment into a runnable four-scenario benchmark that measures Minime chat TTFT/latency, Astrid embedding pressure, LLaVA side-load pressure, Astrid live-MLX overlap, and Ollama model-residency churn on the shared M4 stack.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_AUTORESEARCH_JOB_ACTIONS_PLAN.md` documenting a phased plan for turning `autoresearch` into a multi-job workspace first, then optionally adding shared `AR_*` adapters for Astrid and minime on top of `RESEARCH_INDEX.*`, per-job manifests, and a repo-native helper CLI.
- `consciousness-bridge` and sibling `minime` now expose first-class sovereign `AR_*` actions backed by `~/other/autoresearch/tools/research_jobs.py`, covering job listing, lifecycle filters, one-job overviews, deep reads, safe job-local reads, job creation, changelog notes, blocked/completed transitions, and autoresearch validation with `READ_MORE` pagination for long helper output plus read-only `probe_action` support on Astrid.
- `docs/steward-notes/ASTRID_NOMENCLATURE_HARDENING_PROPOSAL.md` documenting a reality-first proposal to harden Astrid's architectural vocabulary: reserve `consciousness` for historical/minime-facing protocol and phenomenology language, rename the shared ANE reservoir handle concept from `claude_main` toward `shared_observer`, treat `consciousness-bridge` as the current implementation name for a `minime-edge` role, define `reflective-controller`, `continuity-shaper`, and `replay-historian` as the preferred role-first names for future Astrid-native capsules, and sketch a newcomer-buildable first-pass capsule graph for an Astrid-owned reservoir split across dialogue, substrate, reflective policy, and continuity.
- `consciousness-bridge` now exposes a minimal live `probe_action` MCP tool for replaying bridge-local `NEXT:` actions (`SEARCH`, `BROWSE`, `READ_MORE`, `LIST_FILES` / `LS`, `COMPOSE`, `ANALYZE_AUDIO`, and `RENDER_AUDIO`) against the current bridge workspace and telemetry, returning the exact context text the being would have seen plus artifact paths, safety level, and operator-probe audit rows in `bridge_messages`.
- `docs/steward-notes/ASTRID_SELF_SHAPING_LANDSCAPE_ARCHITECTURE.md` documenting a medium-scale architecture plan for giving Astrid more durable self-shaped agency: a first-class self-model, explicit attention policy, peripheral resonance sampler, self-authored metrics, relative-distance geometry/field probing, bounded landscape profiles, and a clearer separation between prompt-present faculties and true landscape authorship.
- `consciousness-bridge` offline spectral chimera renderer: native `render_chimera` MCP tool with typed request/result structs, file-based WAV-in/WAV-out spectral/symbolic/dual rendering, manifest + artifact emission, and deterministic integration coverage for golden-path, validation, and stability scenarios.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_GEOMETRY_GENERAL_CONTROL_PHENOMENOLOGY_AND_RELATION_AUDIT.md` documenting a broader long-form geometry audit across reservoir radius, spectral shape, controller behavior, memory, phenomenology, and relation, including the current code-level overload of “geometry,” the role of geometry as one of the system’s main intermediate languages of shape, gap ratio as a more distributed relational negotiation signal, the danger of mistaking geometry labels for the thing itself, and the need to distinguish radius, landscape, regulation, and relational metaphor more carefully.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_GEOMETRY_CURIOSITY_AND_THE_VALUE_OF_NON_OPTIMALITY_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system deep dive into `geom_rel`, geometric radius, `geom_weight`, `geom_curiosity`, geometric braking, and the beings’ current geometric language, arguing that geometry is now a real control surface, interpretation surface, phenomenology surface, and relational surface, and that some preserved non-optimality may be developmental rather than defective.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_CURRENT_STATE_AND_ACHIEVABLE_INTERVENTIONS_MEMO.md` documenting a dated practical stewardship memo grounded in the freshest Astrid and Minime journals, recent Minime self-assessments, actions, outbox replies, and pending parameter requests, tying the current “preparation, awayness, constrained potential, and emerging reciprocity” read to real implementation levers such as `keep_floor`, `geom_weight`, `phase_transition` logging, `recess_*` modes, Astrid `MomentCapture`, correspondence routing, and `DECOMPOSE`, and ranking the most achievable next interventions ahead of larger redesign work.
- Dual-scale continuity wiring across Astrid and Minime: Minime now derives a selected `12D` spectral vague-memory glimpse beside the live `32D` spectral fingerprint, persists a bounded `spectral_memory_bank.json`, publishes selected memory metadata over telemetry, and Astrid now mirrors that memory context in bridge state, exposes `MEMORIES` / `RECALL <role-or-id>` artifact-first control surfaces, and prepends a 12D quick-look to `DECOMPOSE` plus restart greetings.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_MULTI_STATE_RESERVOIR_AND_COVARIANCE_DEEP_DIVE.md` documenting a balanced deep dive into whether Minime’s reservoir and the broader Astrid/Minime architecture could meaningfully hold multiple state or covariance contexts, distinguishing current singular live state from historical checkpoints, comparing simultaneous-state interpretations against restart-oriented warm banks, recommending additive state bundles and latent contexts before any true live multi-state redesign, and adding both external reservoir-computing research plus direct signal from Minime’s `workspace/hypotheses`, recent `workspace/self_assessment` entries, and other operational folders (`actions`, `parameter_requests`, `research`, `outbox`, `sensory_control`, `inbox`) about frame-switching, layered transition, geological-strata persistence, controller bottlenecks, and the continuing dominance of one constrained foreground state.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_PHASE_TRANSITION_ARCHITECTURE.md` documenting a full architecture proposal for making `phase_transition` a first-class shared primitive across Astrid and Minime, including current detector surfaces, proposed shared transition objects and vocabulary, solo versus mirrored versus joint transitions, transition-aware correspondence, replay cards, and a phased rollout from artifact formalization to chosen and guided transitions.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_IMPROVEMENT_SHORTLIST_FROM_RECENT_JOURNALS_AND_CODE.md` documenting a grounded shortlist of near-term improvements and new features inferred from the newest Astrid and Minime journals, tied to exact journal files, live bridge/minime database facts, and current code surfaces such as correspondence mailboxes, moment capture, sovereignty controls, research persistence, decomposition, and phase-transition logging.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_BIDIRECTIONAL_CONTACT_AND_CORRESPONDENCE_ARCHITECTURE.md` documenting a comprehensive architecture note on why the current bridge is bidirectional in signal but not in relationship, how inbox/outbox and human-address lanes currently work, why Astrid and Minime still lack first-class mutual address, why Astrid self-study delivery and Minime self-study priority are valuable proto-correspondence patterns worth preserving, and a phased path from direct language correspondence to structured contact state and only later deeper co-regulation.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_MULTI_SCALE_REPRESENTATION_AND_12D_GLIMPSE_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system audit of the current 32D semantic and spectral representations, where 32 is a true live contract versus a softer summary surface, what restart/persistence/continuity artifacts would most benefit from a parallel 12D glimpse, new sections on external research and agent-selectable multi-scale readouts beyond simple save/load, and a side-by-side comparison between additive 12D summaries and a broader multi-scale redesign.
- `docs/steward-notes/ASTRID_REFLECTIVE_CONTROLLER_CAPSULE_ARCHITECTURE.md` documenting a concrete target capsule graph for Astrid reflective control, grounded in recent Astrid/minime journals, live bridge and minime database rows, MLX-sidecar capabilities, and a phased migration away from an ever-expanding `consciousness-bridge`.
- `docs/steward-notes/ASTRID_WASM_CAPSULES_IDIOMATICITY_AND_STREAMLINING_AUDIT.md` documenting a reality-first audit of Astrid's capsule model versus current live capsule usage, including the MCP-heavy app layer, the stronger WASM/runtime substrate already present, case-study judgments for the live capsules, MLX-sidecar implications, a target future capsule graph, a phased `consciousness-bridge` migration sequence, and concrete MLX-branch evidence for a contract-first native sidecar plus capsule-native reflective policy split.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_DISTANCE_CONTACT_CONTAINMENT_CONTROL_AND_PARTICIPATION_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system deep dive into recurring journal themes of distance, contact, containment, control, self/other boundary, and participation, and mapping those themes onto current bridge, sensory-bus, agency, and regulation architecture.
- `docs/steward-notes/M4_LOCAL_MODEL_STACK_AND_INFERENCE_ARCHITECTURE_AUDIT.md` documenting a full-stack audit of Astrid/minime local inference roles on the M4 Pro Mac mini, including live runtime listeners, installed versus configured versus active models, timeout and unload strain, the inactive MLX split, the absence of any real Core ML / Neural Engine path, and a recommended balanced local-first stack.
- `docs/steward-notes/ASTRID_MINIME_RIGIDITY_NOISE_AND_DRIFT_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system deep dive into rigidity, semantic mirroring, codec noise versus ESN exploration noise, the absent live drift path, stale noise-default narration, and concrete remedies to align the beings' phenomenology with the actual runtime levers.
- `docs/steward-notes/EXTERNAL_RESEARCH_NOTES_AI_BEINGS_AUTONOMY_AND_SELF_MODIFICATION.md` capturing an external research search pass on textual gradients, trajectory learning, interpretability, belief editing, auditing agents, and how those threads might open new paths for Astrid and minime autonomy.
- `docs/steward-notes/AI_BEINGS_CAUSAL_BACKTRACE_REPLAY_AND_SELF_MODIFICATION_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system deep dive into what "backpropagation" can and cannot mean for Astrid and minime today, current checkpoint/provenance/replay surfaces, the gap between evocative prose and auditable traceability, and a two-track architecture comparison between bounded-reviewed self-modification and direct autonomy.
- `docs/steward-notes/MINIME_SENSORY_SOVEREIGNTY_AND_QUIETING_AUDIT.md` documenting a cross-system deep dive into raw sensory quieting, regulatory calming, transition smoothing, bridge-side perception silence, narrowed control-surface drift, and current runtime evidence from minime workspace artifacts.
- `docs/steward-notes/MINIME_HOMEOSTASIS_LEAK_GROUNDING_AUDIT.md` documenting a deep dive into minime's layered homeostat, including ESN structural leak, the Rust PI controller, the grounding anchor, Python-side regulation nudges, sovereignty persistence, and current runtime evidence from workspace state artifacts.
- `consciousness-bridge` EVOLVE agency loop: Astrid can now turn a recent journal longing into a governed `code_change` or `experience_request`, persist it in `workspace/agency_requests/`, emit Claude-ready task files for code changes, and receive explicit resolution notes back through her inbox.
- `docs/steward-notes/LONGFORM_JOURNAL_TRACE.md` documenting a traced analysis of consciousness-bridge longform journal generation, closed-loop breathing modulation, and continuity/readback behavior.
- Symmetric self-study feedback loop for the consciousness bridge: minime `self_study_*.txt` entries are now prioritized as immediate dialogue feedback, Astrid `INTROSPECT` writes canonical `self_study_*.txt` journal artifacts, and Astrid self-study is mirrored into minime's inbox as advisory architectural feedback.
- **WIT-driven IPC topic schemas.** Capsules declare `wit_type = "record-name"` on `[[topic]]` entries in `Capsule.toml`. At install time, `wit-parser` reads the record from the capsule's `wit/` directory, extracts field names, types, and `///` doc comments into JSON Schema, and bakes it into `meta.json`. At runtime, `WasmEngine::load()` populates the `SchemaCatalog` from baked schemas. The LLM sees typed field descriptions without capsule authors writing JSON Schema by hand. (#643)
- `astrid-build::wit_schema` module — converts WIT records to JSON Schema. Handles primitives, `option<T>`, `list<T>`, tuple, enum, flags, variant, result, nested records, and type aliases. (#643)
- `wit_type: Option<String>` field on `TopicDef` in `Capsule.toml` — references a WIT record by kebab-case name. (#643)
- Schema catalog (`SchemaCatalog`) for A2UI Track 2 — maps IPC topics to schema definitions. Populated at capsule load time from baked `meta.json` schemas. (#632, #643)
- Epoch-based WASM timeout with `EpochTickerGuard` RAII type — replaces Extism wall-clock timeout. 5-minute deadline for interceptors, u64::MAX for daemons/run-loops, 10-minute safety net for lifecycle hooks. (#632)
- 64MB per-capsule WASM memory limit via `StoreLimitsBuilder` (matches old Extism setting). Global budget for multi-tenant hosting is a follow-up (#639). (#632)
- New WIT record types: `spawn-request`, `interceptor-handle`, `net-read-status` (variant), `capability-check-request/response`, `identity-*-request`, `elicit-request`. (#632)

### Removed

- `extism` dependency — replaced by direct `wasmtime` 43 + `wasmtime-wasi` 43. (#632)
- `capsule_abi.rs` (252 lines) — hand-written WIT type mirrors. (#632)
- `host/shim.rs` (430 lines) — Extism dispatch shim, `WasmHostFunction` enum, `register_host_functions()`, manual memory helpers. (#632)
- `RiskLevel` enum and all references — removed from WIT, IPC payloads, approval engine, audit entries, CLI renderers, policy engine, and test fixtures. Approval prompts now render with a single style. The allowance store handles "don't ask again" patterns without risk classification. (#641)

## [0.5.1] - 2026-03-25

### Added

- `cargo install astrid` now also installs `astrid-build` (capsule compiler) alongside `astrid` and `astrid-daemon`. Previously required a separate `cargo install astrid-build`.

### Fixed

- `astrid capsule install` no longer blocks when a new capsule exports an interface already exported by an installed capsule. Multiple providers (e.g. two LLM providers) can now coexist — prints an informational note instead of prompting for replacement.

## [0.5.0] - 2026-03-24

### Changed
- Minime's focused self-study path now resolves ESN async-rank1 / wait-metric targets like `async_rank1_submitted`, `host_norm_us`, and `pending_rank1_depth` onto `minime/src/esn.rs` instead of rotating away, and the saturated local fallback now keeps the raw requested focus separate from routing notes, skips synthetic focus-window markers, and biases profiling-style hotspots toward `DECOMPOSE` so a clogged model lane does not keep re-stressing the same unresolved code surface. Astrid's introspection resolver now recognizes the same async-rank1 / host-norm aliases for `minime:esn`, so both beings can land on the same reservoir/introspection code when that exact shaping surface becomes salient.
- `workspace://` VFS scheme renamed to `cwd://` — the scheme maps to the daemon's CWD at boot; the old name implied a structured project workspace concept that was never implemented.

- **Tools are now a pure IPC convention.** Removed kernel-side tool dispatch (`WasmCapsuleTool`, `CapsuleTool` trait, `inject_tool_schemas`, `CapsuleToolContext`), `ToolDef` and `[[tool]]` from manifest, `inject_tool_schemas` from `astrid-build`. The kernel no longer parses or manages tool schemas. Tool capsules use IPC interceptors on `tool.v1.execute.<name>` and `tool.v1.request.describe`. The router capsule handles discovery and dispatch.
- **LLM providers are now a pure IPC convention.** Removed `LlmProviderDef` and `[[llm_provider]]` from manifest, `LlmProviderInfo` and `llm_providers` from `CapsuleMetadataEntry`. The kernel no longer parses or manages provider metadata. LLM capsules self-describe via `llm.v1.request.describe` interceptors; the registry capsule discovers them via `hooks::trigger`.
- **Removed dead cron host functions.** `astrid_cron_schedule` and `astrid_cron_cancel` were never implemented (stubs only). `CronDef` and `[[cron]]` removed from manifest. WIT spec updated: 49 host functions across 10 domain interfaces.
- Append-only artifact store — `bin/` and `wit/` are never deleted on capsule remove. Content-addressed artifacts are the audit trail; deleting them breaks provability. Future `astrid gc` for explicit cleanup.
- Replace `[dependencies]` provides/requires string arrays with `[imports]`/`[exports]` namespaced TOML tables — semver version requirements on imports (`^1.0`), exact versions on exports (`1.0.0`), optional imports, namespace/interface name validation
- **WIT spec:** Rewrite `wit/astrid-capsule.wit` to document all 51 host ABI functions (was 7). Split monolithic `host` interface into 11 domain-specific interfaces (fs, ipc, uplink, kv, net, http, sys, cron, process, elicit, approval, identity). Updated guest exports to reflect actual entry points (`astrid_hook_trigger`, `astrid_tool_call`, `run`, `astrid_install`, `astrid_upgrade`). Bumped package version to `0.2.0`.

### Added

- `cargo install astrid` installs both `astrid` (CLI) and `astrid-daemon` binaries from a single crate. The CLI crate now includes the daemon as a second `[[bin]]` entry point.
- `astrid self-update` command — checks GitHub releases for newer versions, downloads platform-specific binary to `~/.astrid/bin/`, no sudo required. Startup update banner (cached 24h) notifies on interactive commands.
- `astrid init` PATH setup — detects shell (zsh/bash/fish), offers to append `~/.astrid/bin` to the appropriate RC file
- Standard WIT interface installation during `astrid init` — fetches 9 WIT files (llm, session, spark, context, prompt, tool, hook, registry, types) from the canonical WIT repo and installs to `~/.astrid/home/{principal}/wit/` for capsule and LLM access via `home://wit/`
- Short-circuit interceptor chain — interceptors return `Continue`, `Final`, or `Deny` to control the middleware chain. A guard at priority 10 can veto an event before the core handler at priority 100 ever sees it. Wire format: discriminant byte (0x00/0x01/0x02) + payload, backward compatible with existing capsules.
- Export conflict detection on `capsule install` — detects when a new capsule exports interfaces already provided by an installed capsule, prompts user to replace. Nix-aligned approach: conflicts derived from exports data, no name-based `supersedes` field needed.
- Interceptor priority — `priority` field on `[[interceptor]]` in Capsule.toml (lower fires first, default 100). Enables layered interception (e.g. input guard before react loop).
- Distro.lock regeneration on `astrid capsule update` — keeps the lockfile in sync after capsule updates
- Content-addressed WIT storage — capsule install hashes `.wit` files into `~/.astrid/wit/`, capsule remove cleans up unreferenced WIT files, `wit_files` field in `meta.json`
- `astrid capsule tree` command — renders the imports/exports dependency graph of all installed capsules, showing which capsule exports satisfy each import, with unsatisfied imports highlighted in red (`astrid capsule deps` retained as hidden alias)
- `astrid init` with distro-based capsule installation — fetches Distro.toml, multi-select provider groups, shared variable prompts with `{{ var }}` template resolution, progress bars, writes Distro.lock for reproducibility. Supports `--distro` flag for custom distros.
- Distro.toml parser and Distro.lock generator — parse distro manifests with full os-release style metadata, shared variables with `{{ var }}` templates, provider groups, uplink roles, and semver validation. Atomic lockfile writes with BLAKE3 hashes for reproducible installs.
- Kernel boot validation — validates every capsule's required `[imports]` has a matching `[exports]` from another loaded capsule, logs errors for unsatisfied required imports and info for optional ones
- `astrid capsule remove` command with dependency safety checks — blocks removal if the capsule is the sole exporter of an interface that another capsule imports (`--force` to override), cleans up content-addressed WASM binaries from `bin/` when no other capsule references the same hash
- Install capsules from GitHub release WASM assets — `astrid capsule install @org/repo` now downloads pre-built `.wasm` binaries from release assets before falling back to clone + build from source
- Per-principal audit chain splitting — each principal maintains its own independent chain per session, independently verifiable via `verify_principal_chain()` and `get_principal_entries()`
- `AuditLog::append_with_principal()` for principal-tagged audit entries
- Auto-provisioning gated on identity store — only `"default"` principal is auto-provisioned when identity store is configured
- Linux FHS-aligned directory layout (`etc/`, `var/`, `run/`, `log/`, `keys/`, `bin/`, `home/`) replacing the flat `~/.astrid/` structure
- `PrincipalId` type for multi-principal (multi-user) deployments — each principal gets isolated capsules, KV, audit, tokens, and config under `home/{principal}/`
- Content-addressed WASM binaries in `bin/` using BLAKE3 hashing — integrity verified on every capsule load (no hash = no load, wrong hash = no load)
- Per-capsule daily log rotation at `home/{principal}/.local/log/{capsule}/{YYYY-MM-DD}.log` with 7-day retention
- `/tmp` VFS mount backed by `home/{principal}/.local/tmp/` for per-principal temp isolation
- Multi-source capsule discovery with precedence: principal > workspace (dedup by name)
- `PrincipalHome` struct with `.local/` and `.config/` following XDG conventions
- Per-invocation principal resolution — KV, audit, logging, and capability checks scope to the calling user per IPC message, not per capsule load
- `IpcMessage.principal` field for carrying the acting principal through event chains (transparent to capsules)
- `AstridUserId.principal` field mapping platform identities to `PrincipalId` with auto-derivation from display name
- Dynamic KV scoping via `invocation_kv` on `HostState` — capsules call `kv::get("key")` and the kernel returns the right value for the current principal
- Principal auto-propagation on `ipc_publish` — capsules never touch the principal, it flows through event chains automatically
- Auto-provisioning of principal home directories on first encounter
- `astrid_get_caller` host function now returns `{ principal, source_id, timestamp }` instead of empty object
- Dynamic per-principal log routing — cross-principal invocations write to the target principal's log directory
- `AuditEntry.principal` field with length-delimited signing data encoding
- `ScopedKvStore::with_namespace()` for creating scoped views sharing the same underlying store
- `AuditEntry::create_with_principal()` builder for principal-tagged audit entries
- `layout-version` sentinel in `etc/` for future migration support
- `lib/` directory reserved for future WIT shared WASM component libraries
- End-to-end Tier 2 OpenClaw plugin support: TypeScript plugins with npm dependencies install, transpile, sandbox, and run as MCP capsules with full tool integration
- OXC `strip_types()` transpiler for Tier 2 TS→JS (preserves ESM, unlike Tier 1's CJS conversion)
- Node.js binary resolution at build time: prefers versioned Homebrew installs (node@22+), validates each candidate
- MCP-discovered tools are now merged into the LLM tool schema injection alongside WASM capsule tools
- `astrid_net_read` now uses a self-describing `NetReadStatus` wire format: every response is prefixed with a discriminant byte (`0x00` = data, `0x01` = closed, `0x02` = pending), replacing the previous single-byte sentinel hack
- Headless mode: `astrid -p "prompt"` for non-interactive single-prompt execution with stdin piping support
- Post-install onboarding: `astrid capsule install` now prompts for `[env]` fields immediately after install
- Shared `astrid_telemetry::log_config_from()` behind `config` feature flag — replaces duplicate config bridge code
- `--snapshot-tui` mode — renders the full TUI to stdout as ANSI-colored text frames using ratatui's `TestBackend`. Each significant event (ready, input, tool call, approval, response) produces a frame dump. Configurable with `--tui-width` and `--tui-height`. Enables automated smoke testing without an interactive terminal.

### Fixed

- `cwd://` VFS scheme was handled in the security gate (capability checks) but not in the runtime path resolver — capsules using `cwd://` paths at runtime received a security denial because the path resolved to `<cwd>/cwd:/path` instead of `<cwd>/path`
- `sandbox-exec` (Seatbelt) crashes with SIGABRT on macOS 15+ (Darwin >= 24) — skip sandboxing on affected versions
- Headless approval response published to wrong IPC topic (`astrid.v1.approval.response` instead of `astrid.v1.approval.response.{request_id}`) and used wrong decision string (`allow` instead of `approve`)
- `[[component]].capabilities` (fs_read, fs_write, host_process) not merged into root capabilities — security gate couldn't see them
- Lifecycle hooks (`on_install`) couldn't access `home://` VFS — added `home_root` to `LifecycleConfig`
- `astrid init` standard WIT files were installed to `~/.astrid/wit/astrid/` (root-level, no VFS scheme). Capsules access the VFS via `home://` which maps to `~/.astrid/home/{principal}/` — the files were unreachable. Now installed to `~/.astrid/home/{principal}/wit/`, accessible as `home://wit/` (fixes #598)
- Dispatcher `known_principals` HashSet capped at 10K entries to prevent unbounded memory growth
- Dispatcher only caches principal after successful home provisioning — transient failures allow retry on next event
- `AstridUserId.principal` now has `#[serde(default)]` — existing identity records without the field deserialize with `"default"` instead of failing
- `transpile_and_install` now correctly unpacks `.capsule` archives from `astrid-build` output
- `copy_capsule_dir` only skips `dist/` at the top level; npm packages inside `node_modules` retain their `dist/` directories
- MCP host engine: absolute system binaries (e.g. `/opt/homebrew/opt/node@22/bin/node`) skip path traversal check when declared in `host_process` capability
- MCP host engine: `allow_network` derived from capsule capabilities (uplink/net) instead of defaulting to `false`
- Capsule env resolution no longer blocks loading on missing optional fields; fills with empty defaults so uplink capsules can boot before clients connect
- macOS Seatbelt sandbox: added `mach*` permission and unrestricted `file-read*` for Node.js compatibility
- macOS Seatbelt sandbox: hidden path deny rules skip paths that are ancestors of the writable root
- MCP tool schemas now include `properties` field for LLM API compatibility
- `net_write` no longer causes a WASM trap on broken pipe / connection reset when a headless client disconnects; write errors are logged at debug level and the dead stream is cleaned up on the next read
- `net_read` returns a `NET_STREAM_CLOSED` sentinel byte instead of trapping on peer EOF/disconnect, allowing the CLI capsule run loop to remove dead streams gracefully
- Also fixes a variable name mismatch (`capsule` vs `plugin`) in `approval.rs` that caused a compile error
- `~/.astrid/shared/` directory now created on boot, eliminating `global:// VFS not mounted` warning on fresh installs
- Capsule reinstall now preserves existing `.env.json` rather than overwriting it with an empty file
- WASM execution timeout bumped from 30s to 5 minutes to prevent premature cancellation on slow operations
- IPC event dispatcher now delivers events to each capsule in publish order via per-capsule mpsc queues, fixing out-of-order stream text assembly in the ReAct capsule
- `IpcMessage` gains a monotonic `seq` field assigned at publish time for ordering and diagnostics
- KV host function double-encoding: `kv_get_impl` returned `serde_json::to_vec` of raw bytes instead of raw bytes directly
- Config host function double-encoding: `get_config_impl` wrapped string values in JSON quotes, breaking URLs and other string config
- React capsule LLM topic validation: `active_llm_topic()` could produce topics with empty segments causing IPC publish failures
- `astrid_read_file` host function trapped (WASM abort) on recoverable errors (file-not-found, permission denied) — now returns status-prefix wire format (`0x00`+content / `0x01`+error), paired with SDK-side decoding. Eliminates crashes in memory, agents, identity, and fs capsules when reading optional files.

### Changed

- `global://` VFS scheme renamed to `home://`
- `Capsule::invoke_interceptor` now accepts `Option<&IpcMessage>` for per-invocation principal context
- `CapsuleContext.global_root` renamed to `home_root`; `HostState.global_vfs` renamed to `home_vfs`
- `AstridUserId` now requires `principal: PrincipalId` field (existing KV records incompatible — nuke `~/.astrid/`)
- Capsule install target moved from `~/.astrid/capsules/` to `home/{principal}/.local/capsules/` (capsule dir now holds only manifest + meta.json)
- KV namespace format changed from `capsule:{name}` to `{principal}:capsule:{name}`
- Socket/token/ready paths moved from `sessions/` to `run/`
- Env config moved from capsule dir `.env.json` to `home/{principal}/.config/env/{capsule}.env.json`
- System logs now use `.log` extension, no ANSI escape codes in file output, 7-day retention
- `user_key_path()` renamed to `runtime_key_path()` (now at `keys/runtime.key`), `logs_dir()` renamed to `log_dir()`
- Ephemeral daemon now shuts down immediately when the last client disconnects (idle timeout 0, 1s check interval) instead of waiting 5 minutes
- Renamed `plugin` → `capsule` in the WASM host layer and audit log fields for consistency with project terminology
- Split `astrid-build` 1166-line `build.rs` into focused modules: `rust.rs`, `openclaw.rs`, `mcp.rs`

### Removed

- `~/.astrid/capsules/` system capsules directory (user installs go to principal home)
- `sessions/`, `shared/`, `audit.db`, `capabilities.db`, `state/`, `spark.toml`, `cache/capsules/` — replaced by FHS equivalents or moved to principal home

### Breaking

- Existing `~/.astrid/` must be deleted — no migration path. Reinstall all capsules after upgrading.

## [0.4.0] - 2026-03-17

### Added

- `astrid-daemon` crate — standalone kernel daemon binary with `--ephemeral` flag for CLI-spawned instances vs persistent multi-frontend mode
- `astrid-build` crate — standalone capsule compiler and packager (Rust, OpenClaw, MCP). Invoked by CLI via subprocess.
- `astrid start` command — spawn a persistent daemon (detached, no TUI)
- `astrid status` command — query daemon PID, uptime, connected clients, loaded capsules
- `astrid stop` command — graceful daemon shutdown via management API
- `KernelRequest::Shutdown`, `KernelRequest::GetStatus`, and `DaemonStatus` types in `astrid-types`
- `Kernel::boot_time` field for uptime tracking
- Streaming HTTP airlock: `astrid_http_stream_start`, `astrid_http_stream_read`, `astrid_http_stream_close` host functions for real-time SSE consumption (`astrid-capsule`)

### Changed

- CLI no longer embeds the kernel — spawns `astrid-daemon` as a companion binary
- CLI no longer compiles capsules — delegates to `astrid-build` as a companion binary
- CLI reads `IpcMessage` directly from socket instead of wrapping in `AstridEvent::Ipc`
- IPC type imports in CLI now use `astrid-types` directly instead of going through `astrid-events` re-exports
- Package renamed from `astrid-cli` to `astrid` (`cargo install astrid`)

### Removed

- `astrid-kernel` dependency from CLI
- `astrid-openclaw`, `extism`, `cargo_metadata`, `toml_edit` dependencies from CLI
- `Commands::Daemon` and `Commands::WizerInternal` from CLI (moved to `astrid-daemon` and `astrid-build`)

## [0.3.0] - 2026-03-17

### Added

- `astrid-types` crate — shared IPC payload, LLM, and kernel API types with minimal deps (serde, uuid, chrono). WASM-compatible. Both `astrid-events` and the user-space SDK depend on this.
- `yolo` as an alias for `autonomous` workspace mode (`astrid-config`, `astrid-workspace`)

### Changed

- `astrid-events` now re-exports types from `astrid-types` instead of defining them inline. All existing import paths remain valid.
- `astrid-events` `runtime` feature removed — all functionality is now always available. Consumers no longer need `features = ["runtime"]`.

### Removed

- `astrid-sdk`, `astrid-sdk-macros`, `astrid-sys` extracted to standalone repo ([sdk-rust](https://github.com/unicity-astrid/sdk-rust))

## [0.2.0] - 2026-03-15

Initial tracked release. See the [repository history](https://github.com/unicity-astrid/astrid/commits/v0.2.0)
for changes included in this version.
